**INT. GILLEY’S BEDROOM – 2:19 AM**

No music. No voices. Just the humid tangle of skin and breath and muffled gasps.

A garage lamp slices through the blinds — thick, golden slats across the bed, the walls, the curve of **KATHY**’s spine as she rides **GILLEY** with slow, grinding precision. Her body gleams with sweat. Her thighs flex, muscles tight, hair damp and wild around her face.

She’s naked, unabashedly. No hesitation. No coyness. Her tits bounce with each shift of her hips, slick and luminous in the low light, as if they’re performing alongside her. Front and center. Their own silent audience.

**KATHY**   (low, breath ragged)  
 Don’t say a fucking word.

**GILLEY** (barely audible)  
 Not a syllable.

His hands hover, then land — palms sliding from her waist to her hips, unsure if he’s guiding or being guided. He’s shirtless, damp, his chest rising fast. The scent of his aftershave — cheap, stubborn — hangs in the air like an old joke.

The room creaks. The bedframe groans. Every sound amplified by the silence between them.

**KATHY** (dry, clipped)

**GILLEY**  (strained, eyes half-lidded)

**KATHY**

Her eyes flicker — not to him, but somewhere just past him. Her mouth is parted like she’s tasting a memory. Her body is here, completely, every movement deliberate. But her mind’s lagging behind, like it hasn’t caught up to the fact that it’s **GILLEY**’s hands gripping her, **GILLEY**’s body beneath hers, not—

Not who?

She closes her eyes tighter, grinds again. Deeper. Her nipples brush his chest, wet and hard and insistent.

**GILLEY** (gritted)

(beat)

But maybe I’ll fuck you again.

That line lands hard. **GILLEY** falters. His rhythm stutters. His breath catches, not from pleasure, but from something heavier — something hot and confusing and far too intimate.

She’s sweating like she just walked off stage. Her inner thighs are slick with grool. Her breath is choppy. Her skin smells like smoke, salt, and adrenaline. And there’s a look on her face — not passion. Not satisfaction.

Displacement.

**GILLEY (V.O.)**    
She’s been wet for three hours.  For me.  Because of the show.  What a high! 

Her movements become more frantic. Less measured. She’s chasing something. Not climax. Not even contact.

A correction.

**KATHY (V.O.)**    
This should feel like a victory.  It doesn’t.  It feels like misfiring the last firework in the box.

**GILLEY** watches her — really watches. Her flushed skin. Her clenched jaw. The way her hands claw the sheet beside his head instead of touching him. The way her breasts bounce, not like an invitation, but a distraction.

And he knows. She’s not in his bed. She’s in her own head. And maybe — just maybe — in someone else’s arms.

**INT. GILLEY’S BEDROOM – 2:49 AM**

Silence again.

**KATHY** is sprawled across the bed, limbs splayed, hair damp, skin cooling under the lazy swipes of a broken ceiling fan. Her chest rises and falls slowly, rhythmically. Spent.

**GILLEY** lies beside her, flat on his back, one arm tucked behind his head, the other reaching down under the sheets.

He winces slightly. Then casually peels off the condom — no ceremony, no thought — and tosses it toward the wastebasket.

It *misses*, landing with a quiet, wet slap on top of a spiral notebook next to his amp.

**CAMERA CLOSE-UP:  
** The notebook — smudged, bent, pages dog-eared — reads *“Setlists / **KATHY**’s Riffs – DO NOT TOUCH”* in **KATHY**’s handwriting.

He doesn’t notice. Or doesn’t care.

**GILLEY**  (low)

(beat)

You realize what we did tonight?

**KATHY** (sighs)

**GILLEY** (smiling)

(beat)

We killed it. W.O. Wright’s. We actually pulled it off.

(beat)

Big Mike handed me a can full of quarters like it was a goddamn Grammy.

**KATHY** 
Hey, that can pay for at least one Mountain Dew and two Slim JIMs. We’re basically famous.

**GILLEY** 
I’m serious, though.

(beat)

We weren’t just okay. We were… good.   Like, better than we had any right to be.

**KATHY** (quietly)

(beat)

Not polished. Not tight. But alive.

**GILLEY**
Exactly.

(beat)

There was a Moment — when we were halfway through *“Sunday Bloody Sunday”* — I looked out, and for like, two seconds? Everyone in that room was locked in. Actually listening. Not just drinking. Not just waiting. Like… in it.

**KATHY** 
I saw it too.

(beat)

Thought I was imagining it.

**GILLEY** 
We gave ‘em something they didn’t expect.

**KATHY** 
Which, in that bar, is saying something.

(beat)

I think we have to do it again.

**GILLEY** 
We will. Two weeks.

(beat)

You in?

**KATHY** 
Of course I’m in.

She rolls away from him, turning to her side. Not cold. Not angry. Just done with the Moment — with *this* Moment.

**KATHY **(CONT’D)**  
But next time?  Let’s maybe not do Phil Collins again.

**GILLEY**(deep breath)  
No promises.

A long beat.

**JEFF (V.O.)**    
They wouldn’t talk about the sex.  Not tomorrow. Not next week.  Maybe never.
But that night?  They both knew it wasn’t about love.  It was about making something loud.

**CAMERA PUSHES IN on the notebook on the floor.**  
A string of ink smeared from the used condom draped across the cover.

Something important, now marked. And soon, remembered.
